FACET_message[061204,00/04]: ["ele_pads4u.elib","SML# 2001-0111","14 Feb 2001","Jonathan Gainsley","Sun Microsystems Laboratories - Publicly Released","0.35u process pad library for Electric","------------------------------------------------------------------","Description:  A set of simple pads for use with the Electric VLSI","Design System, designed for the 0.35u process.","This pad library has been released for public use by","Sun Microsystems Laboratories, see SML#2001-0077.  It is free","of any Sun Microsystems propriatary information.","------------------------------------------------------------------","*** Please email any bug fixes/improvements to jonathan.gainsley@eng.sun.com ***","","","NOTE1:  Pads do not have ESD protection","NOTE2:  1 lambda = 0.2 microns","NOTE3:  Pads conform to MOSIS 4 metal submicron DRC rules (SCN4M_SUBM),","        available at www.mosis.org (rules are subject to export restrictions)","","","Included Pads:","","PAD_raw:         Raw pad, also for use with analog inputs","PAD_vdd:         Clean VDD pad","PAD_gnd:         Clean GND pad","PAD_dvdd:        Dirty VDD pad","PAD_dgnd:        Dirty GND pad","PAD_inbuf:       Input pad","PAD_out:         Output pad","PAD_io:          I/O pad","PAD_flwout:      High speed but low voltage source follower output pad","PAD_corner:      Corner pad","PAD_spacer:      Spacer pad","PAD_halfSpacer:  Half-sized spacer pad","","","Pad Usage:","","Pads are designed to be spaced 750 lambda apart.  Each has a facet center in ","the same spot, so spacing pad A at (0, 0), and pad B at (750, 0) will line up ","the pads properly next to each other.  A corner_pad is placed 375 lambda from ","its adjacent pads.","","Each pad has 6 exports, 3 on each side for dvdd, dgnd, and the well tap ","boundary.  Placing pads at the proper spacing puts ports from adjacent pads ","on top of each other.  Tools -> Routing -> Auto Stiching will then connect ","them."]
